< text>
Pretty campus. Lots of paths through the campus where the kids can explore on bikes. Great activities for the kids in the camps run by UC Berkeley in the summer. I've been here for conferences, too, and the facilities are nice. However, there is not very much bicycle parking, especially not around the conference hall, and I've always ended up locking my bike to the railing.< /text>

<gmap_id>0x80857c333efbb2db:0x6974bcb0d7022b15< /gmap_id>< rating>
4</rating>
< text>
Clark Kerr is a beautiful place to live, and the commute, while far, is often exaggerated. There's lots of natural scenery, big rooms and lounges, and it's adjacent to student-accessible track, pool, tennis courts, volleyball pits, and hiking trails. And it is surrounded by a similarly beautiful neighborhood that makes you feel as though you are frequently separated from the chaos of the UC campus. This, however, comes with a downside of feeling isolated from the campus activity and prone to staying in your dorm room rather than getting out and involved at school.
All in all, the one serious downside to Clark Kerr is the uniquely antisocial atmosphere. Certain cliques -- primarily the athletes and the frat/sorority rushers -- dominate the dorms in a homogeneous and unaccepting way. It's difficult to avoid them, and it can get annoying if you do not fit nicely into them. There certainly aren't as many hardcore STEM kids here; it's generally more a party culture kind of group, if you're into that.
Living here for a third year now, so there is definitely a net benefit. But you need to be prepared for the kinds of exclusive crowds you encounter here. Of course, there will be decent kids, but it's definitely a different kind of group predominating here.<//text>

< text>
BRING CASH FOR YOUR TIPS. They don't have an option to tip on your card.

I needed my nails done and decided to take a risk on this place despite the less than preferable amount of stars. I have to say, I actually really liked it! They are more expensive than most places I have gone before but I think I'm willing to pay it if my nails hold up well. They dip powder us a little thicker than I'm used to but my nail tech didnt file my nails down to paper thin like many techs do. She also did not cut me with the file (HUGE pet peeve of mine), nor did she let the dremel heat up my nail to the paint of burning.

All in all, my tech was quiet and didn't give me any time to pick out the nail color I wanted so I was looking through the ring with one hand while she worked on the other, but she was efficient so I don't mind. This was the first place I have gone that offered dip powder designs and I have to say, I'm very happy with it! I will watch them and see how they wear and grow out in the next few weeks. If they hold up well, I will be back!</text>

<Response>None< /Response>< Text>
I really wanted to like this place. The reviews seemed great and it was close to our hotel.  We ordered hamburgers, one combo avocado bacon cheese burger with tater tots and one cheese burger non combo. We seated ourselves outside and waited and waited and waited for our food. There was a large party in front of us so I'm assuming that's what took so long but it took a long time. We got our drinks 30 mins after we sat down and then our food about 40 mins in. Our order came out a little wrong which happens they gave use fries instead of tater tots and said they would switch it for us. We started on our hamburgers which were really good and cooked perfectly, but even after we finished our burgers our tots still weren't out. I went to the counter and they were sitting there, had been for a bit because they were cold. There was another table that got some items of their order wrong as well. I could tell the staff was a little frazzled but were trying. If it's crowded be prepared to wait and have patience. So all in all the food was good, the staff was nice but got frazzled during a not so busy afternoon.<//Text>

My husband and I stopped in here for a late lunch one day, when it seemed that everything else in the area was closed. When he brought out our cups of water, I noticed a black thing floating in one of the cups and before I could say anything, he stuck his finger in the water and dragged it out on the side of the cup and set the cup down on the table!?!? I was introduced to this store 40 years ago and have consistently trusted Roger Stuart Clothes for my slacks, sport coats, suits, a tuxedo, silk shirts, socks and belts. <date>1458754945580< /date><rating>5</rating>< Review>
I have been going to Roger Stuart for 30 years.  And my father went there probably since they opened.

They are the LAST of the REAL manufacturers that sell their own quality private label items.  They also sell a lot of other items that are mass produced and cheaper.  I don't shop at any other store in the Garment District for suits.  It would be a waste of time.  This is the place.

Insider tip: Ask to go to the "Back Room" for the highest quality suits!

Most of the staff are men who have been in the trade for generations.  Some are in their 70s and still selling suits.  Great guys, with stories to tell.

They have been around longer then anyone else because they have been doing right since the beginning.

Anytime I am in L.A. it's a destination.</Review>

<date>1533243402550<//date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
I know Dennis Prager slightly, and Roger Stuart clothes is a long time advertiser of his. When I needed a new suit for a wedding, I decided, just for the heck of it, to make the trip downtown.

It was worth it, even with having to pay $12 for parking.

The store itself is clean, well set up and easy to shop in. And the helpful and knowledgeable sales staff makes it even better. My sales person, Robert Fisher was a total pro and helped me find exactly what I wanted for less than I was prepared to pay, and I wound up with a wonderful high quality all wool Italian suit  for less than $300 including tax.

Speaking of which, RSC only handles all wool, top quality stuff, no polyester blends or other crap. There are indeed places you can get a suit for less, but it won't be of this kind of quality. Given what RSC is selling, this is incredible value for money.

Some things to know...while RSC can set you up with someone to do alterations, like most other places you pay extra. Unlike most other places, it's not an in house tailor, which I actually prefer since I have a great tailor and I have found that a lot of the in house tailors in these places just aren't all that good. You are better off with your own tailor.

Next, parking is easily available right next door to the store. There's a $12 maximum, but the lot is secure and well run, and it's not too bad for something in the middle of the garment district, since you might want to browse in other shops and get a little more mileage for your $12. There is a store next to the parking lot that validates with purchase, so maybe you could buy something cheap like a tie or a belt,  and then hit RSC, although I didn't do that.

Anyway, I had a great experience at RSC. I will definitely be going back. They earned every one of those five stars.<//Text>

< review>
I found my new eyeball health home!

I used to wear glasses many years ago. When it started getting more difficult to read things close up, I knew I would have to find an eye doctor. With so many choices, I thought the decision would be difficult. Then I found Dr. Larsson!

Compassionate, understanding, informative, kind, fun...do you expect these things in your eye doctor? You should, and if you do, Dr. Kathryn Larsson and her competent, professional staff are your one-stop-shop for better vision.

In my appointment today, I came away understanding more about my vision issues than I thought possible. She kindly explained every test she was doing, what they are designed to find out about my eyes, and she even decided to do some different tests based on our conversation. (She's responsive to what she learns about you, to ensure you get the best treatment!)

With large pictures of her beautiful family on her wall, she is clearly a dedicated mother, wife, and friend, and I appreciate knowing those little details about my doctors. I imagine she would be fantastic with kids, as she's had several of her own!

Finally, her staff was friendly, down-to-earth, and understanding. I was almost late for my appointment, and they were still just as friendly as I could have hoped for, and when it came time to select frames, they were understanding of what my insurance covered and made recommendations with an eye to what they would cost out of pocket. I was so satisfied with how I was treated here!

Well, folks, I wear glasses again. But thanks to Visionary Optometry, the prospect isn't at all disheartening. I look forward to routine eye exams! Thank you, Kathryn!<//review>

< text>
The good:
Some very friendly, professional, and helpful employees like Adriana, Erika, Paul, Ngoc, Jenna, Alex, Ngoc, Victor and Rose. The store lines are usually fast and most items are in stock. I'm always glad when I see Erika in the aisles because she gives good advice. And Adriana always greets me when she sees me. Paul is fast and very knowledgeable.

The bad:
The pharmacy's pick up times are usually 30 minutes to an hour for most of my drop offs. The pick up lines can sometimes be super long. The store is usually dusty and certain shelves are confusing with sticker prices or merchandise not in the correct place. A lot of the front end cashiers don't greet even if they are not busy. Paul is fast but too in a hurry. Sometimes it triggers an anxious feeling.< /text>

<userid>106841842659951904620< /userid><name>Nick Doty (Nick)< /name><time>1621443672972< /time><rating>2< /rating><text>When the lockers work, they work fine. They send you a text/email saying you have a package, you go pick it up. Easy enough.

<Date>1583793981724<//Date><Rate>5<//Rate><Review>These lockers are fantastic.

They're keyless entry, so you just input the code you get in the text/email or scan the QR code and it disengages the lock on the box that your package is in. Then you just grab your stuff and close the locker. You also usually get the pickup code for the locker before most package trackers tell you that the package has been delivered, which is great since some carriers don't mark the package as delivered until the driver returns from their route. So it can save you time that would otherwise be spent waiting for that delivery update. On the rare occasions that the driver didn't get a drop off code, they'll just bring your package straight to your door or follow any delivery instructions you may have set up.

If you're like me and have that constant low key paranoia that someone is going to steal your package, whether it's due to past experiences or just because that's the way you are, then these lockers are a great thing to have in your building. Knowing that your stuff will be safe and secure until you're able to go get it really cuts away that stress and worry that stems from other delivery methods.

I've yet to have a negative experience with Luxer One, and I doubt that I will. So if your apartment complex is considering having Luxer One Lockers installed, you should encourage them to do so. Your online shopping experience will be greatly improved by having them.< /Review>< pics>
None</pics>

<rate>5< /rate><Text>Recently moved into an apartment complex in Southern California that uses Luxer One parcel lockers. I had been using Amazon Lockers for about 6 months prior to this, so the concept was familiar.

So far, can't say I have any complaints. There's an online portal that you can access and it will let you know if you have any packages waiting, and you can also see the history of previous packages, as well as images when the carrier delivers the package, and a signature of the person who picks it up.

You can set up your account with your phone and email, and when you receive a package, you'll receive a text and/or email with a pick up code, or a link to a QR code.

Go to the Luxer One station, input your code or scan your QR code, and your locker will automatically pop open and you can collect your package.

This may vary from location to location, but there is an "oversized" locker which is shared. First time I encountered it was interesting. I was given a message to only take my package, and when I opened the locker door, I saw my package in there along with maybe 5 others. Bit of a trust system with that, but I didn't have any issues.<//Text>< Pictures>

< Review>
RESIDENTS BE AWARE!! Luxer one claims to be a smart and secure solution to package management, BUT this is not true!! ---------- My apartment management uses luxer one, as a resident I have no choice. My package was stolen last week,  one person used an amazon carrier code to open a shared locker and stole two packages. Wow, this is very scary and concerning: 1. poor carrier management system: drivers from the same carrier share same code, and the carrier code doesn't expire; 2. luxer one doesn't have any two way authentication (from the conversation with customer service, they don't even care), so basically anyone with the code can open the locker;  3. luxer one doesn't want to be responsible for any stolen package, nor do they care... I'd suggest stay away from them at all costs!</Review>

<Name>Bruce Andrews<//Name><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Really like the Luxer package system. Feel good to know that my packages that are delivered by FedEx, UPS, or DHL are secured instead of being left at door, (especially high value,or things that are targets for theft)
To retrieve  them, you must enter the code that is either texted, or Emailed to you. Then you have to sign the touch pad tp have the door to seperate bins open to get package out.
Unsure if package room is monitored by CCTV by Luxer also.
Our unit also has one large bin for items that will not fit in the smaller bins.
This bin usually contains items for numerous tennants ,and as with the other bins you must enter access code  and sign in.
If I have a particular package that has high value, you can notify carrier not to put it in the large bin, or make other arrangements for secure delivery.
The only downside  to this sustem is that it sometimes takes a awhile  to recieve the access code. The apartment complex is able to look up codes if needed.< /Review>

I love Luxor One. I dont have to stress about being home for a delivery, missing a delivery, or getting home before the office closes to pick up a delivery. I live in an apartment complex. High risk of theft if a package is left at my door.

However, the only courier service that will use it is USPS. Fed Ex delivers to the door and so does UPS. They say it is because they have to deliver to the address on the package, not to a locker.
